2434ATC TL
       An improper value is specified as the TL command value.
       Indexing a tool not mounted on the turret was attempted with
       the TL command. 
       The sequence restart function was used to restart a program 
       which incorporates a TL command for indexing a tool number not
       mounted in the turret.
         TL:Tool number index command 
          (TL = &&$$%%, 
           where && is the nose R compensation No.,
       	  $$ is the tool No.   and 
       	  %% is the tool offset No.)
       Or, the order of edge-number was larger than the number of
       tool-edges. (for the spec of "Many chips tool")
       Or, in the case of "TOOL OFFSET 999" spec and "MULTI EDGE TOOL" 
       spec, tool number were not the following ranges.
          MULTI-TOOL  8-EDGES:1-210 or 281-999 
          MULTI-TOOL 12-EDGES:1-210 or 321-999 
       [Code]
        Ordered Tool-number.
        FFFFFFFF->In TOOL-ID spec
        When the edge-number was ordered, code was "edge & holder-number
        (HEX)".
       [Measures to Take]
        When conducting a sequence restart, ensure that the tools
        mounted in the turret match the tools specified in the program.

2466Synchronization M-code
       Improper designation of synchronization M code (M100).
       [Object]SYSTEM
       [Code]
       164->M100 is designated in the tool nose radius compensation
       mode.
       2XX->For A and B turrets, different synchronization M codes are
       designated.
       XX:Hexadecimal number of the designated M code (This alarm does
       not occur actually.)
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)Part program
       While the NC is in the wait state by M100, the program is not
       prefetched. If, however, nose R compensation is activated, M100
       cannot be specified because that nose R compensation requires
       advanced program reading.
       2)For the standard software, no M code other than M100 can be
       specified as a command for waiting synchronization. This mean
       the alarm indicated by the code 2XX will not occur.
       Program Example
       [Code]164
       N100 G41 G01 X100 F1
       N101 M100
       [Measures to Take]Eliminate M100 from nose R compensation
       function active portion.

2475W-axis command G-code
       The G code (G122 or G123) designating on which side, A or B,
       the W-axis command should be given is designated for other than
       sub-spindle specification models.
       It instructed in G code (G122,G123) in the tailstock mode 
       by a Sub spindle-tailstock Control specification.
       It instructed in G code (G122,G123) in the tailstock mode 
       by a W axis Cut-tailstock Control specification.
       [Object]SYSTEM
       [Code]Hexadecimal number of the designated G code
       [Probable Faulty Locations]Program error
       Program Example:
       G13   G14
       G123  G123
       :     G0 W100
       :     :
       [Measures to Take]Delete G122 or G123 from the program.

       	  at the synchronization tap cycle of a continuous
       	  block.
       Others->Hexadecimal number of designated LD value
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       Faulty program (compound fixed cycle block)
       Program Example1:
        G178 X40 Z80 C0 I46 F40 L30 LD=-10
       		   <- It is outside the range.
        G178 X40 Z80 C0 I46 F40 L30 LD=0.001
       		   <- It is smaller than the parameter value.
       Program Example2:
        G178 X50 Z50 F=100 K10 L20	     <- There is no LD value.
             X70 Z30		     LD=10   <- There is LD value.
       [Measures to Take]
       Check the LD command in the compound fixed cycle block.
       G178 X40 Z80 C0 I46 F40 L30 LD=10
       [Related Specifications]Multi-machining model

       except for Y-axis was performed before moving YS-axis to
       turning-position.

          YS-axis was not in the turning-position of

       2->After changing the spindle-mode, the movement-command
          except for Y-axis was performed before moving YS-axis
          to turning-position.

         program-end.

         setting turning-position.

         turning-position Y-axis.

       4)Add G00-command to move turning-position of Y-axis.
         ex:

2663Turning cut condition error of CAS 
       A necessary condition is insufficient in case of the turning cut.
       [Charecter-string]None
       [Code]
       1-> It tried to rotate the work spindle in states other than 
       YI=0 (main axis center), and to execute the cutting feed.
       2-> It tried to rotate the spindle in the state that YS axis 
       graphic zero point of the CAS system parameter is not 
       corresponding to the [TURNING POSITION] parameter value and to 
       execute the cutting feed.
       3-> It tried to rotate the main axis with the amount of a wick high 	
        (YS axis) correction exceeds 1mm, and to execute the cutting feed.
       [Expected faulty point]
       Please confirm the NC program.
       Moreover, in the case of code=2, the [TURNING POSITION] setting 
       value was changed when this machine adjusts it is thought. 
       Please confirm the YS graphic zero point setting value and 
       the [TURNING POSITION] setting values.
       In the case of code=3, when the amount of a wick high (YS axis) 
       correction exceeds 1mm, the interference detection cannot be done.
       [Treatment measures]
       To execute it after it positions it in YI=0, the turnig cut 
       (The cutting feed is done by rotating the work spindle) corrects 
       the processing program.
       Moreover in the case of code=2, It is changed so that 
       YS graphic zero point setting value may agree with 
       the [TURNING POSITION]	setting value by turning off the power 
       and turn it back on again. In old soft version, it is not changed
       automatically. Please the same value as the [TURNING POSITION] 
       setting value is set to YS axis graphic zero point in Slant 
       Y axis specification machine.
       It is necessary to confirm graphic zero point setting value 
       of other axises, after adjusting the machine.
       In the case of code=3, Please cancel CAS function with M867,and 
       process it after confirming no interference.

2703Chucking miss

       condition unsatisfied.

          given, the air pressure switch failed to come ON.
       2->When the chucking error detection ON command was given, the
          pressure switch input had been ON.
       3->The grip limit switch did not correctly function when the
          grip confirmation unit was advanced by a chucking miss
          sensor ON command (M133).
       4->Though Tailstock chucking error detection ON command (M433)
          was given, the air pressure switch failed to come ON.
       5->Though 2nd chucking error detection ON command (M633)
          was given, the air pressure switch failed to come ON.
       6->Tailstock tool chucking error detection ON command(M1191)
          was given, the air pressure switch failed to come ON.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       Workpiece is not clamped in the chuck correctly.
       [Measures to Take]
       Check the workpiece chucked condition.

2705Tailstock quill over advance
       Over advance of the tailstock spindle(alarm level of this
       alarm
       is alarm A if it occurs during execution of a main program*.)
       Bit data status of I/O check NO.27 INPUT:
       bit5=0->iTSRTC
       bit4=0->iTSLMC
       bit3=1->iTSOAC
       * Refer to Alarm A 1748 Tailstock spindle over advance.
       [Code]
       1->The tailstock spindle has over advanced to actuate the
          over advance confirmation LS.
       2->The tailstock spindle over-advanced to
       the in-position LS was OFF.
       3->In the case of NC tailstock spcification, the tailstock
          spindle over-advanced and the workpiece hold confirmation
          LS turned OFF.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)The mounted workpiece is shorter than the specified length.
         (Operation error)
       2)The tailstock moved from a distant position and, therefore,
         hit the overtravel limit switch before reaching the
         workpiece.
       3)The tailstock advance command was issued without mounting
         a workpiece. (Operation error)
       [Measures to Take]
       1)Re-position the tailstock closer to the workpiece, or adjust
         the dog position.
       2)Designate the tailstock spindle advance command only after
         setting a workpiece in the chuck.
2706Polygon cutting command condition
       Polygon cutting ON/OFF command (M221/M220) is given when the
       conditions for polygon cutting are not satisfied.
       [Object]SYSTEM
       [Code]
       1->Spindle zero speed signal is not input.
       2->Spindle in-stop signal is not output.
       3->Spindle rotation command is active.
       4->The M-tool spindle rotation command (SB command) is active.
       5->The M-tool spindle is rotating.
       6->C-axis is in the jointed state.
       7->During M221 - M226 polygon cutting command execution, other
          polygon cutting mode is directly designated without
          designating cancel command (M220).
       8->A polygon cutting command is designated in the M241 (M-tool
          spindle; 1st range) mode.
       9->The main spindle chuck and the pickoff chuck are closed.
       10->In ATC specification, flat turning instruction was
           performed by the state which milling tool station does not
           have divided.
       11->It is in spindle extreme low speed rotation mode.
       12->It is in Main spindle low speed acceleration mode.
       13->Turret does not clamp.
       14->Any of M220 to M226 commands was issued at the G14
           (saddle B) side.
       15->The G14 (saddle B) side was in synchronous cutting
           rotation mode.
       17->In synchronous hobbing mode.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)Program error
         Designate M221/M220 after the rotation command of the
       spindle
         or the M-tool spindle.
       2)Operation error
         In the MDI mode, M221/M220 is input after the rotation
         command of the spindle or the M-tool spindle.
       3)Due to incorrect EC input status, representing the spindle
         rotation condition, the spindle rotation condition cannot be
         judged correctly.
       4)The spindle or the M-tool spindle is forcibly rotated by an
         external factor.
       Program Example:
         M03 S500
         M221
          :
       [Measures to Take]
       1)Correct the program.
       2)Check the M-tool spindle speed.
         "Sb" on the block data display screen.

2711Door open
       A spindle rotation command is designated with the machine door
       opened while the VAC motor is being prepared for operation.
       Normally, if a spindle rotation command is designated while
       the
       VAC motor is being prepared for operation, alarm D 4213 "VAC
       motor not ready to start" will occur.  The spindle will start
       after the operation preparation completion signal is turned
       on.
       It is however very dangerous if the spindle starts with the
       machine door opened.  To prevent it, this alarm occurs so that
       the spindle does not start even when the door interlock is
       OFF.
       When the door interlock is ON, alarm A 1304 "Door interlock"
       will occur.
       [Object]SPINDLE, M-TOOL SPINDLE
2712ATC no spec.
       On the machine without ATC function, an ATC related command
       was
       issued.
       [Object]SYSTEM
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)Programming error
         On the machine without ATC function, M06 or M228 command was
         issued.
       2)Operation error
       Program Example:
         M228, M06
       [Measures to Take]
       Delete M228, M06 commands from the program.

       TL: Tool number index command (TL = &&$$%%, where && is the
       nose R compensation No., $$ is the tool No. and %% is the

2716ATC TL

       restart a program which incorporates a TL command for indexing
       a tool number not mounted in the turret.
       TL: Tool number index command (TL = &&$$%%, where && is the
       nose R compensation No., $$ is the tool No. and %% is the
       tool offset No.)
       [Code]XXYYZZ

       YY:Tool number
       ZZ:Tool Offset number

       program.

2720M06/M228 command disable
       M06, M228, or MG command was wrongly specified.
       M06: Tool change command
       M228: ATC next tool return command
       MG: Magazine index command (MG = **, where ** is the magazine
       pot No.)
       [Object]Turret
       [Code]X
       1->M06 was specified though the next tool was not ready.
       2->M228 was specified though the next tool was not ready or
          the tool return operation was not ready to start.
       3->M06 was specified without positioning the turret in the
          tool change position.
       5->An MG command was issued with a sequence number that
          inhibits magazine indexing.
       6->M06 command was issued during a tool calling or storing
          movement.
       7->M228 command was issued during a tool calling or storing
          movement.
       8->M06 was specified though a long boring tool was
          mounted in the turret H1.
       9->M06 command was issued during an AAC cycle.
       10->M06 command was issued when Measurement sensor unit
           is not in retract position.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)By LB35II-MATC-Y LU45-MATC-Y, a next tool preparation state
         is ATC operation sequence number 12 and 49. By
       LB15II-MATC-Y,
         a next tool preparation state is ATC operation sequence
         number 8 and 51. They are going along M06 instructions that
         ATC operation sequence number is not a next tool preparation
         state.
       2)By LB35II-MATC-Y LU45-MATC-Y, a tool return operation start
         state is ATC operation sequence number 27 and 68.
         By LB15II-MATC-Y, a tool return operation start state is ATC
         operation sequent number 23 and 65. They are going along
       M228
         instructions that ATC operation sequence number is not a
       tool
         return operation start state.
       3)M06 was issued though the turret is not indexed at the tool
         change position.
       5)For LB15II/LB35II-MATC-Y and LU45-MATC-Y, MG commands can be
         issued with the ATC operation sequence number 1, 2, 41, and
         42. An MG was issued with a sequence number other than
         1, 2, 41,or 42.

2726Magazine encoder read

       position encoder.
       [Code]
       1->Magazine
2727Magazine turn condition
       A magazine rotation command was issued though the magazine
       rotating conditions are not met.
       [Code]XX
       9->The sub arm is not in position for enabling magazine
          rotation.
       10->The tool extraction pin at the magazine manual tool
       loading
           /unloading position is not set at clamp position.
       11->For tool ID specification, the tool ID data reading arm is
           not in retract position.
       12->A magazine pot is not unclamp.
       13->There is not a magazine pot in a frontal  change position.
       14->There is exchange arm in EAMG position.
       17->For tool ID specification, the tool attachment is
           not in data read position (left position).
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       9)For LB35II-MATC-Y and LU45-MATC-Y, magazine rotation is
         possible only when the sub arm is in the RS position or
         directed to the RS. While the sub arm is in any other state,
         the magazine cannot rotate.
       10),11)Magazine rotation is not possible in either of the
         following cases:
         the tool extraction pin at the magazine manual tool
         loading/unloading position is not set at clamp position,
         or the tool ID data reading arm is not in retract position.
       12),13),14) By LB15II-MATC-Y, a magazine pot is unclamp and is
         a frontal change position, and when there is exchange arm in
         EAMG position, it can be done magazine rotation.
2728Magazine tool number
       The input signal status sent from the magazine tool presence
       confirmation proximity switch provided at the magazine ATC
       position does not correspond to the data of the magazine pot
       indexed to the magazine ATC position set on the "*ATC MAGAZINE
       INFORMATION*" screen in the tool data setting mode.
       [Object]SYSTEM
       [Code]X
       1->Although the "*ATC MAGAZINE INFORMATION*" screen shows the
          tool data, the magazine tool presence confirmation
       proximity
          switch is OFF.
       2->Although the "*ATC MAGAZINE INFORMATION*" screen does not
          show the tool data, the magazine tool presence confirmation
          proximity switch is ON.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       The "*ATC MAGAZINE INFORMATION*" screen displays the tool
       mounted in each magazine pot. For the magazine pot indexed to
       the magazine ATC position, therefore, the presence/absence of
       tool data on "*ATC MAGAZINE INFORMATION*" screenshould always
       match the input signal status sent from the magazine tool
       presence confirmation proximity switch.
       However, data setting error on the screen, malfunction of the
       proximity switch, or disconnection of the signal wire will
       cause mismatch between tool data setting and input signal
       status, resulting in this alarm.
2729Magazine no return pot
       The tool cannot be returned because there is no empty pot.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       The magazine has no empty pot. Tool data is wrongly set on the
       "*ATC MAGAZINE INFORMATION*" screen in tool data setting mode.
       When setting the tool diameter, note that a large diameter
       tool
       requires two empty pots arranged side by side while an extra
       large diameter tool requires three consecutive pots. To shows
       the empty pot, the "*ATC MAGAZINE INFORMATION*" screen shows
       0 at the tool number files. Also note that a dummy pot does
       not mean an empty pot.
       The magazine has no reserve pot, when the magazine is FIX
        pot specification.
2730Tool insert disable
       Tool pot for return tool is not available if a tool is
       inserted
       into the pot at the insertion station.
       [Code]
       1->The tool cannot be inserted into the tool pot.
       2->The tool cannot be mounted to the turret.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       Operation error
       Operation Example:The tool number write button is pressed.
       [Measures to Take]
       Prepare the tool pot for return tool.
       For a super-large tool, three pots are required in succession.
       For a large tool, two pots are required in succession.
       [Related Specifications]
       ATC

        3->MT command was executed in a position other than the ATC
           start position.
        4->MT=0 command was issued during an ATC cycle.
        5->MT=0 command was issued in a position other than the ATC
           start position.
        6->The tool number specified with a MT command is duplicated
           in the pot/tool correspondence table.
        7->The tool number specified with a MT command is not
           registered in the pot/tool correspondence table.
        8->Cover tool attaching/detaching command is not fit
           to cover tool condition.
        9->Lathe tool cycle command or milling tool cycle command is
           not fit to cover tool condition.
       [Measures to Take]
        If the above code is 2, execute T00 command in MDI mode.
        If the other code appears, check the program and the
        "pot/tool correspondence table" in tool data setting mode.

       AT commands are not used properly.
       [Code]

        3->AT command for the AAC was executed without locating the
           AAC in the AAC start position.
